4395<div>

4396<h2>

4397Why You Should Choose Dark Cabinets for Your Home</h2>

4398

4399

4400<p>

4401Dark cabinets provide a classy, ageless look for your kitchen. Depending on your color and design choices, dark cabinets work well with modern, rustic, transitional, or kitchens of any style. Choose between stained or painted cabinets to achieve the ideal look for your kitchen.</p>

4402

4403

4404<h2>

4405<br />

4406

4407Benefits of Dark Kitchen Cabinets</h2>

4408

4409

4410<ul>

4411

4412 <li>

4413Add Luxury</li>

4414

4415 <li>

4416Hide Scratches and Spills</li>

4417

4418 <li>

4419Versatile Style</li>

4420

4421</ul>

4422

4423

4424<p>

4425<br />

4426

4427Ready to incorporate the mood and depth of dark cabinets into your kitchen renovation? A daring color choice can increase the warmth and lavishness of your home&nbsp;in a very cost-effective way. Dark cabinets are an innovative and bold kitchen design idea for any size remodel.</p>

4428

4429

4430<h2>

4431<br />

4432

4433Dark Kitchen Cabinet Benefits</h2>

4434

4435

4436<p>

4437<strong>

4438Add Luxury</strong>

4439</p>

4440

4441

4442<p>

4443Dark cabinets add luxury you can&rsquo;t find in stock or builder-grade kitchens. This is because dark kitchens feel more custom than a set of standard cabinets. Choosing dark&nbsp;<a href="https://vevano.com/resource-center/cabinet-finishes/" target="_blank">

4444cabinet finishes</a>

4445&nbsp;influences the mood of your kitchen, making the space feel intimate and cozy, no matter the shade from<a href="https://vevano.com/page/gray-kitchen-cabinet-collections/">

4446&nbsp;<u>

4447grey kitchen cabinets</u>

4448</a>

4449&nbsp;to brown kitchen cabinets. Kitchen d&eacute;cor and furnishings can transform the ambiance from formal to edgy as the richness of dark kitchen cabinets spans either mood.</p>

4450

4451

4452<p>

4453<strong>

4454Hide Scratches and Spills</strong>

4455</p>

4456

4457

4458<p>

4459Darker colors hide imperfections better than lighter colors. If you whack a white cabinet door with a waffle maker, you&rsquo;re bound to see a ding. With a dark cabinet, the tone hides and blends the dent rather than highlighting it. Dark kitchen cabinets also show fewer signs of aging than lighter options; cracks, scratches, and sun exposure are more forgiving on darker&nbsp;<a href="https://vevano.com/resource-center/wood-kitchen-cabinet-types/" target="_blank">

4460types of wood cabinets</a>

4461. If you have pets and kids, it&rsquo;s much harder to keep white cabinets looking clean. Dark kitchen cabinets allow you to clean less frequently, and it takes less effort to make your kitchen look tidy.</p>

4462

4463

4464<p>

4465<strong>

4466Versatile Style</strong>

4467</p>

4468

4469

4470<p>

4471Dark shades aren&rsquo;t just for&nbsp;<a href="https://vevano.com/resource-center/modern-kitchen-ideas/" target="_blank">

4472modern kitchens</a>

4473. Many interior design styles gain panache from darker colors.&nbsp;<a href="https://vevano.com/resource-center/modern-farmhouse-kitchen-design-ideas/" target="_blank">

4474Farmhouse kitchens</a>

4475&nbsp;look great with a darker wood island paired with a lighter countertop and subway tile backsplash. Contemporary kitchens benefit from dark grey cabinetry with clean lines and high contrasts. Dark brown wood cabinets evoke comfort and coziness in classic or traditional kitchens. The options are endless.</p>

4476

4477

4478<h2>

4479<br />

4480

4481Which Dark Cabinet Shade is Best for Your Kitchen?</h2>

4482

4483

4484<p>

4485The &ldquo;dark&rdquo; in your dark cabinets comes from either a stain or paint. Both types can look similar from a distance, but with a stain, you notice the grain of the wood and other intricate details as you look closer, such as variations in the color. Choose a stained cabinet if you prefer seeing the unique grain of wood. But if you&rsquo;d rather not see the wood grain, choose a painted cabinet in any shade for balanced and even color throughout.</p>

4486

4487

4488<p>

4489Shades are also available in different colors from dark grey to dark brown. Grey is a slightly lighter tone in warm or cool shades. Brown is a warmer tone, reminiscent of<a href="https://vevano.com/page/wood-kitchen-cabinet-collections/">

4490&nbsp;<u>

4491wood kitchen cabinets</u>

4492</a>

4493&nbsp;but with a darker, more modern ambiance.</p>

4494

4495

4496<h2>

4497<br />

4498

4499What Countertops and Floors Go with Dark Cabinets?</h2>

4500

4501

4502<p>

4503For dark cabinets, we recommend lighter colors for other elements in your kitchen. The contrast of light and dark is interesting and keeps the space from feeling too gloomy or dim.</p>

4504

4505

4506<p>

4507<strong>

4508Countertops:</strong>

4509&nbsp;Nearly any countertop choice works well with dark cabinets, but lighter colors provide a nice contrast while medium colors blend well. Avoid overly dark countertops with dark cabinets, as both shades can make your kitchen feel smaller and crowded. Marble, quartz, or granite countertops are both ideal materials for your kitchen remodel.</p>

4510

4511

4512<p>

4513<strong>

4514Wall Colors:</strong>

4515&nbsp;Use color on your walls to highlight the beauty of your cabinets and countertops. This works best by using softer, lighter colors that make dark cabinets pop. You can also go with a bright splash of color. Pairing a dark cabinet with a fun blue, green, or yellow wall creates a fun atmosphere with high visual interest.</p>

4516

4517

4518<p>

4519<strong>

4520Backsplash:</strong>

4521&nbsp;Backsplash ideas range from bright and colorful to plain and minimal. Your choice of kitchen backsplash provides a chance to highlight your style and personality. If you love farmhouse kitchens, choose a subway tile backsplash in a lighter color to contrast nicely with your dark cabinetry. Colorful accents such as a bright geometric tile or solid red are also fun ideas for your new kitchen.</p>

4522

4523

4524<p>

4525<strong>

4526Flooring:</strong>

4527&nbsp;As with other elements in your kitchen, contrast is key. A lighter floor adds the ideal contrast with dark cabinets. LVT, hardwood, or tile all work well with dark&nbsp;<a href="https://vevano.com/resource-center/cabinet-door-styles-101/" target="_blank">

4528cabinets of any style</a>

4529&nbsp;and design.</p>

4530

4531

4532<p>

4533<strong>

4534Lighting:</strong>

4535&nbsp;Since dark colors absorb more light than they reflect, adding more lighting sources to brighten up your space is a great idea. Lights with glass shades or large multi-light fixtures are great additions. Under-cabinet lighting also brightens up counter space under wall cabinets to create a more open look.</p>

4536

4537

4538<p>

4539<strong>

4540Appliances:</strong>

4541&nbsp;While contrast is often the goal with interior designs, a stark contrast can be too distracting. As such, most appliance colors and finishes work well with dark cabinets but be careful of the stark contrast created when pairing bright white appliances with dark cabinets. We recommend stainless steel appliances or other neutral colors if your cabinets are especially dark.</p>

4542

4543

4544<h2>

4545<br />

4546

4547Dark Cabinet Hardware Choices</h2>

4548

4549

4550<p>

4551Choosing cabinet hardware is a critical part of completing the look you want to achieve, as well as ensuring your cabinets are functional. When pairing the pulls and knobs with your dark cabinets, the style is less important than the finish. The shape and style are open to your personal aesthetics, but the finish is key towards determining whether the hardware goes with the dark color or not.</p>

4552

4553

4554<p>

4555The right finish adds character and charm to a kitchen or bathroom while a poor match stands out, but not in a good way. We recommend finishes such as stainless steel, satin gold, oil-rubbed bronze, or antique pewter, as these add the right amount of polish and balance out your darker kitchen cabinetry with a lighter metal.</p>

4556

4557

4558<h2>

4559<br />

4560

4561FAQs About Dark Kitchen Cabinets</h2>

4562

4563

4564<p>

4565Have some questions before you buy dark kitchen cupboards? We have answers and many different kitchen cabinet ideas for inspiration.</p>

4566

4567

4568<h3>

4569<br />

4570

4571Are dark wood cabinets coming back?</h3>

4572

4573

4574<p>

4575<a href="https://vevano.com/page/white-kitchen-cabinet-collections/">

4576<u>

4577White kitchen cabinets</u>

4578</a>

4579&nbsp;are currently more popular than dark cabinets, but the darker look is coming back in modern and transitional kitchens. If you don&rsquo;t like the look of a pristine white kitchen but still love trendsetting, a dark kitchen can get you there. Darker cabinets are increasing in popularity because they&rsquo;re easier to care for and add sophistication where lighter paints and natural woods cannot.</p>

4580

4581

4582<p>

4583Where light wood cabinets show more muck and wear-and-tear, darker cabinet colors hide scratches and grime more easily. They&rsquo;re also incredibly chic as darker stains tend to look more custom and posher than standard white cabinets.</p>

4584

4585

4586<p>

4587Wood cabinets themselves, however, are always in style, no matter the shade. Wood features a more pleasing grain than laminate or fiberboard, and comforting and warmer than stainless steel. Wood is a timeless, classic&nbsp;<a href="https://vevano.com/resource-center/cabinet-materials/" target="_blank">

4588cabinet material</a>

4589&nbsp;that works in kitchens of any style, from contemporary to farmhouse.</p>

4590

4591

4592<h3>

4593<br />

4594

4595Would a small kitchen look good with dark cabinets?</h3>

4596

4597

4598<p>

4599Usually small kitchens look better in light cabinet colors, but with a few tricks, dark wood cabinets can look stunning in any size kitchen. While light kitchen cabinets have the benefit of reflecting more light (making a room look bigger) kitchens with dark cabinets need other elements to feel light and airy.</p>

4600

4601

4602<p>

4603Small kitchens look good with dark cabinets when paired with light wall colors, a minimalist aesthetic, or light-colored countertops. The lighter elements reflect light and the contrast adds definition and style to small kitchens, where space to display d&eacute;cor is at a premium. Choose gray cabinets rather than black cabinets to help your small kitchen feel less dim and crowded. Dark cabinets in a minimalist style keep your kitchen from looking cluttered and congested, instilling a sense of openness.</p>

4604

4605

4606<h3>

4607<br />

4608

4609Which dark cabinet is right for your kitchen?</h3>

4610

4611

4612<p>

4613The right dark cabinet for your kitchen depends on your style and color preferences. Two of our favorite dark kitchen cabinets have opposite styles and shades. See how they compare to help you narrow down exactly what you love about dark wood kitchen cabinets.</p>

4614

4615

4616<p>

4617<strong>

4618Wilora Paloma Marquis Dark Wood</strong>

4619</p>

4620

4621

4622<p>

4623This collection features<a href="https://vevano.com/product/32035-mdw10x10-marquis-dark-wood-10x10-kitchen/">

4624&nbsp;<u>

4625dark brown kitchen cabinets</u>

4626</a>

4627, with a modern frameless construction. The slab style doors and drawer fronts feature a beautiful dark chocolate wood grain texture. Ideal for modern kitchens, the Marquis Dark Wood cabinets pair well with simple hardware pulls, and metal light fixtures. If you prefer function over form, this collection is designed with storage in mind, the frameless construction allows for more storage space than its framed cabinet counterparts. They&rsquo;re also made of engineered wood which is more water-resistant and warp-resistant than real wood.</p>

4628

4629

4630<p>

4631<strong>

4632Wilora Hawthorne Shaker Cinder</strong>

4633</p>

4634

4635

4636<p>

4637This collection works well in modern or farmhouse kitchens. The more traditional frame style features a&nbsp;<a href="https://vevano.com/resource-center/cabinet-door-styles-101/" target="_blank">

4638Shaker style door</a>

4639&nbsp;with rectangular frames and recessed panels. Each door and frame is stained with a classically comforting grey shade. These<a href="https://vevano.com/product/32040-scc10x10-shaker-cinder-10x10-kitchen/">

4640&nbsp;<u>

4641dark gray cabinets</u>

4642</a>

4643&nbsp;are slightly lighter than dark brown cabinets, so the wood grain is easier to see. If you love a farmhouse kitchen style, but don&rsquo;t care for a hard to clean bright white cabinet, these shaker cabinets create the same look and feel, but with an easier-to-maintain surface.</p>

4644

4645

4646<h3>

4647<br />

4648

4649How can you brighten your kitchen with dark cabinets?</h3>

4650

4651

4652<p>

4653If you love dark wood cabinets, but want a brighter kitchen, there are many design tips to create the ideal kitchen you&rsquo;re looking for.</p>

4654

4655

4656<p>

4657<strong>

4658Open shelving</strong>

4659: Opting for open shelving instead of traditional wall cabinets can make your kitchen space feel brighter and more open. This creates a gradient in your kitchen as colors get darker going from ceiling to floor (if you opt for a dark-colored floor as well).</p>

4660

4661

4662<p>

4663<strong>

4664Under cabinet lighting</strong>

4665: Installing under-cabinet lighting adds light in places natural light rarely touches. Shining focused light on countertops and shelves both brightens and adds mood lighting to your kitchen. Other traditional lighting options are also a good idea, pendant lights over an island or recessed lights throughout your kitchen do so much to brighten up the space.</p>

4666

4667

4668<p>

4669<strong>

4670Two-toned cabinets</strong>

4671: With this method, choose two different cabinet colors: one for the wall cabinets and one for your base cabinets. Traditionally, a darker color is reserved for the base cabinets and a lighter color for the upper cabinets. This lets you achieve the lush look of dark cabinetry but keeps your kitchen bright because the lighter tone of the wall cabinets reflects more light.</p>

4672

A daring color choice can increase the warmth and lavishness of your home\u0026nbsp;in a very cost-effective way. Dark cabinets are an innovative and bold kitchen design idea for any size remodel.\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003ch2\u003e\u003cbr /\u003e\nDark Kitchen Cabinet Benefits\u003c/h2\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eAdd Luxury\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003eDark cabinets add luxury you can\u0026rsquo;t find in stock or builder-grade kitchens. This is because dark kitchens feel more custom than a set of standard cabinets. Choosing dark\u0026nbsp;\u003ca href=\"https://vevano.com/resource-center/cabinet-finishes/\" target=\"_blank\"\u003ecabinet finishes\u003c/a\u003e\u0026nbsp;influences the mood of your kitchen, making the space feel intimate and cozy, no matter the shade from\u003ca href=\"https://vevano.com/page/gray-kitchen-cabinet-collections/\"\u003e\u0026nbsp;\u003cu\u003egrey kitchen cabinets\u003c/u\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u0026nbsp;to brown kitchen cabinets. Kitchen d\u0026eacute;cor and furnishings can transform the ambiance from formal to edgy as the richness of dark kitchen cabinets spans either mood.\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eHide Scratches and Spills\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003eDarker colors hide imperfections better than lighter colors. If you whack a white cabinet door with a waffle maker, you\u0026rsquo;re bound to see a ding. With a dark cabinet, the tone hides and blends the dent rather than highlighting it. Dark kitchen cabinets also show fewer signs of aging than lighter options; cracks, scratches, and sun exposure are more forgiving on darker\u0026nbsp;\u003ca href=\"https://vevano.com/resource-center/wood-kitchen-cabinet-types/\" target=\"_blank\"\u003etypes of wood cabinets\u003c/a\u003e. If you have pets and kids, it\u0026rsquo;s much harder to keep white cabinets looking clean. Dark kitchen cabinets allow you to clean less frequently, and it takes less effort to make your kitchen look tidy.\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eVersatile Style\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003eDark shades aren\u0026rsquo;t just for\u0026nbsp;\u003ca href=\"https://vevano.com/resource-center/modern-kitchen-ideas/\" target=\"_blank\"\u003emodern kitchens\u003c/a\u003e. Many interior design styles gain panache from darker colors.\u0026nbsp;\u003ca href=\"https://vevano.com/resource-center/modern-farmhouse-kitchen-design-ideas/\" target=\"_blank\"\u003eFarmhouse kitchens\u003c/a\u003e\u0026nbsp;look great with a darker wood island paired with a lighter countertop and subway tile backsplash. Contemporary kitchens benefit from dark grey cabinetry with clean lines and high contrasts. Dark brown wood cabinets evoke comfort and coziness in classic or traditional kitchens. The options are endless.\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003ch2\u003e\u003cbr /\u003e\nWhich Dark Cabinet Shade is Best for Your Kitchen?\u003c/h2\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003eThe \u0026ldquo;dark\u0026rdquo; in your dark cabinets comes from either a stain or paint. Both types can look similar from a distance, but with a stain, you notice the grain of the wood and other intricate details as you look closer, such as variations in the color. Choose a stained cabinet if you prefer seeing the unique grain of wood. But if you\u0026rsquo;d rather not see the wood grain, choose a painted cabinet in any shade for balanced and even color throughout.\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003eShades are also available in different colors from dark grey to dark brown. Grey is a slightly lighter tone in warm or cool shades. Brown is a warmer tone, reminiscent of\u003ca href=\"https://vevano.com/page/wood-kitchen-cabinet-collections/\"\u003e\u0026nbsp;\u003cu\u003ewood kitchen cabinets\u003c/u\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u0026nbsp;but with a darker, more modern ambiance.\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003ch2\u003e\u003cbr /\u003e\nWhat Countertops and Floors Go with Dark Cabinets?\u003c/h2\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003eFor dark cabinets, we recommend lighter colors for other elements in your kitchen. The contrast of light and dark is interesting and keeps the space from feeling too gloomy or dim.\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eCountertops:\u003c/strong\u003e\u0026nbsp;Nearly any countertop choice works well with dark cabinets, but lighter colors provide a nice contrast while medium colors blend well. Avoid overly dark countertops with dark cabinets, as both shades can make your kitchen feel smaller and crowded. Marble, quartz, or granite countertops are both ideal materials for your kitchen remodel.\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eWall Colors:\u003c/strong\u003e\u0026nbsp;Use color on your walls to highlight the beauty of your cabinets and countertops. This works best by using softer, lighter colors that make dark cabinets pop. You can also go with a bright splash of color. Pairing a dark cabinet with a fun blue, green, or yellow wall creates a fun atmosphere with high visual interest.\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eBacksplash:\u003c/strong\u003e\u0026nbsp;Backsplash ideas range from bright and colorful to plain and minimal. Your choice of kitchen backsplash provides a chance to highlight your style and personality. If you love farmhouse kitchens, choose a subway tile backsplash in a lighter color to contrast nicely with your dark cabinetry. Colorful accents such as a bright geometric tile or solid red are also fun ideas for your new kitchen.\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eFlooring:\u003c/strong\u003e\u0026nbsp;As with other elements in your kitchen, contrast is key. A lighter floor adds the ideal contrast with dark cabinets. LVT, hardwood, or tile all work well with dark\u0026nbsp;\u003ca href=\"https://vevano.com/resource-center/cabinet-door-styles-101/\" target=\"_blank\"\u003ecabinets of any style\u003c/a\u003e\u0026nbsp;and design.\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eLighting:\u003c/strong\u003e\u0026nbsp;Since dark colors absorb more light than they reflect, adding more lighting sources to brighten up your space is a great idea. Lights with glass shades or large multi-light fixtures are great additions. Under-cabinet lighting also brightens up counter space under wall cabinets to create a more open look.\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eAppliances:\u003c/strong\u003e\u0026nbsp;While contrast is often the goal with interior designs, a stark contrast can be too distracting. As such, most appliance colors and finishes work well with dark cabinets but be careful of the stark contrast created when pairing bright white appliances with dark cabinets. We recommend stainless steel appliances or other neutral colors if your cabinets are especially dark.\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003ch2\u003e\u003cbr /\u003e\nDark Cabinet Hardware Choices\u003c/h2\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003eChoosing cabinet hardware is a critical part of completing the look you want to achieve, as well as ensuring your cabinets are functional. When pairing the pulls and knobs with your dark cabinets, the style is less important than the finish. The shape and style are open to your personal aesthetics, but the finish is key towards determining whether the hardware goes with the dark color or not.\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003eThe right finish adds character and charm to a kitchen or bathroom while a poor match stands out, but not in a good way. We recommend finishes such as stainless steel, satin gold, oil-rubbed bronze, or antique pewter, as these add the right amount of polish and balance out your darker kitchen cabinetry with a lighter metal.\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003ch2\u003e\u003cbr /\u003e\nFAQs About Dark Kitchen Cabinets\u003c/h2\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003eHave some questions before you buy dark kitchen cupboards? We have answers and many different kitchen cabinet ideas for inspiration.\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003ch3\u003e\u003cbr /\u003e\nAre dark wood cabinets coming back?\u003c/h3\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003e\u003ca href=\"https://vevano.com/page/white-kitchen-cabinet-collections/\"\u003e\u003cu\u003eWhite kitchen cabinets\u003c/u\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u0026nbsp;are currently more popular than dark cabinets, but the darker look is coming back in modern and transitional kitchens. If you don\u0026rsquo;t like the look of a pristine white kitchen but still love trendsetting, a dark kitchen can get you there. Darker cabinets are increasing in popularity because they\u0026rsquo;re easier to care for and add sophistication where lighter paints and natural woods cannot.\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003eWhere light wood cabinets show more muck and wear-and-tear, darker cabinet colors hide scratches and grime more easily. They\u0026rsquo;re also incredibly chic as darker stains tend to look more custom and posher than standard white cabinets.\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003eWood cabinets themselves, however, are always in style, no matter the shade. Wood features a more pleasing grain than laminate or fiberboard, and comforting and warmer than stainless steel. Wood is a timeless, classic\u0026nbsp;\u003ca href=\"https://vevano.com/resource-center/cabinet-materials/\" target=\"_blank\"\u003ecabinet material\u003c/a\u003e\u0026nbsp;that works in kitchens of any style, from contemporary to farmhouse.\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003ch3\u003e\u003cbr /\u003e\nWould a small kitchen look good with dark cabinets?\u003c/h3\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003eUsually small kitchens look better in light cabinet colors, but with a few tricks, dark wood cabinets can look stunning in any size kitchen. While light kitchen cabinets have the benefit of reflecting more light (making a room look bigger) kitchens with dark cabinets need other elements to feel light and airy.\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003eSmall kitchens look good with dark cabinets when paired with light wall colors, a minimalist aesthetic, or light-colored countertops. The lighter elements reflect light and the contrast adds definition and style to small kitchens, where space to display d\u0026eacute;cor is at a premium. Choose gray cabinets rather than black cabinets to help your small kitchen feel less dim and crowded. Dark cabinets in a minimalist style keep your kitchen from looking cluttered and congested, instilling a sense of openness.\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003ch3\u003e\u003cbr /\u003e\nWhich dark cabinet is right for your kitchen?\u003c/h3\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003eThe right dark cabinet for your kitchen depends on your style and color preferences. Two of our favorite dark kitchen cabinets have opposite styles and shades. See how they compare to help you narrow down exactly what you love about dark wood kitchen cabinets.\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eWilora Paloma Marquis Dark Wood\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003eThis collection features\u003ca href=\"https://vevano.com/product/32035-mdw10x10-marquis-dark-wood-10x10-kitchen/\"\u003e\u0026nbsp;\u003cu\u003edark brown kitchen cabinets\u003c/u\u003e\u003c/a\u003e, with a modern frameless construction. The slab style doors and drawer fronts feature a beautiful dark chocolate wood grain texture. Ideal for modern kitchens, the Marquis Dark Wood cabinets pair well with simple hardware pulls, and metal light fixtures. If you prefer function over form, this collection is designed with storage in mind, the frameless construction allows for more storage space than its framed cabinet counterparts. They\u0026rsquo;re also made of engineered wood which is more water-resistant and warp-resistant than real wood.\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eWilora Hawthorne Shaker Cinder\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003eThis collection works well in modern or farmhouse kitchens. The more traditional frame style features a\u0026nbsp;\u003ca href=\"https://vevano.com/resource-center/cabinet-door-styles-101/\" target=\"_blank\"\u003eShaker style door\u003c/a\u003e\u0026nbsp;with rectangular frames and recessed panels. Each door and frame is stained with a classically comforting grey shade. These\u003ca href=\"https://vevano.com/product/32040-scc10x10-shaker-cinder-10x10-kitchen/\"\u003e\u0026nbsp;\u003cu\u003edark gray cabinets\u003c/u\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u0026nbsp;are slightly lighter than dark brown cabinets, so the wood grain is easier to see. If you love a farmhouse kitchen style, but don\u0026rsquo;t care for a hard to clean bright white cabinet, these shaker cabinets create the same look and feel, but with an easier-to-maintain surface.\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003ch3\u003e\u003cbr /\u003e\nHow can you brighten your kitchen with dark cabinets?\u003c/h3\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003eIf you love dark wood cabinets, but want a brighter kitchen, there are many design tips to create the ideal kitchen you\u0026rsquo;re looking for.\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eOpen shelving\u003c/strong\u003e: Opting for open shelving instead of traditional wall cabinets can make your kitchen space feel brighter and more open. This creates a gradient in your kitchen as colors get darker going from ceiling to floor (if you opt for a dark-colored floor as well).\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eUnder cabinet lighting\u003c/strong\u003e: Installing under-cabinet lighting adds light in places natural light rarely touches. Shining focused light on countertops and shelves both brightens and adds mood lighting to your kitchen. Other traditional lighting options are also a good idea, pendant lights over an island or recessed lights throughout your kitchen do so much to brighten up the space.\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eTwo-toned cabinets\u003c/strong\u003e: With this method, choose two different cabinet colors: one for the wall cabinets and one for your base cabinets. Traditionally, a darker color is reserved for the base cabinets and a lighter color for the upper cabinets. This lets you achieve the lush look of dark cabinetry but keeps your kitchen bright because the lighter tone of the wall cabinets reflects more light.\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003ch2\u003e\u003cbr /\u003e\nPersonalized\u0026nbsp;Design Service for Your Kitchen Cabinets\u003c/h2\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003eNot sure which style of dark cabinet to choose for your dream kitchen? Choose between stained or painted cabinets to achieve the ideal look for your kitchen.\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003ch2\u003e\u003cbr /\u003e\nBenefits of Dark Kitchen Cabinets\u003c/h2\u003e\n\n\u003cul\u003e\n\t\u003cli\u003eAdd Luxury\u003c/li\u003e\n\t\u003cli\u003eHide Scratches and Spills\u003c/li\u003e\n\t\u003cli\u003eVersatile Style\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cbr /\u003e\nReady to incorporate the mood and depth of dark cabinets into your kitchen renovation? A daring color choice can increase the warmth and lavishness of your home\u0026nbsp;in a very cost-effective way. Dark cabinets are an innovative and bold kitchen design idea for any size remodel.\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003ch2\u003e\u003cbr /\u003e\nDark Kitchen Cabinet Benefits\u003c/h2\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eAdd Luxury\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003eDark cabinets add luxury you can\u0026rsquo;t find in stock or builder-grade kitchens. This is because dark kitchens feel more custom than a set of standard cabinets. Choosing dark\u0026nbsp;\u003ca href=\"https://vevano.com/resource-center/cabinet-finishes/\" target=\"_blank\"\u003ecabinet finishes\u003c/a\u003e\u0026nbsp;influences the mood of your kitchen, making the space feel intimate and cozy, no matter the shade from\u003ca href=\"https://vevano.com/page/gray-kitchen-cabinet-collections/\"\u003e\u0026nbsp;\u003cu\u003egrey kitchen cabinets\u003c/u\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u0026nbsp;to brown kitchen cabinets. Kitchen d\u0026eacute;cor and furnishings can transform the ambiance from formal to edgy as the richness of dark kitchen cabinets spans either mood.\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eHide Scratches and Spills\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003eDarker colors hide imperfections better than lighter colors. If you whack a white cabinet door with a waffle maker, you\u0026rsquo;re bound to see a ding. With a dark cabinet, the tone hides and blends the dent rather than highlighting it. Dark kitchen cabinets also show fewer signs of aging than lighter options; cracks, scratches, and sun exposure are more forgiving on darker\u0026nbsp;\u003ca href=\"https://vevano.com/resource-center/wood-kitchen-cabinet-types/\" target=\"_blank\"\u003etypes of wood cabinets\u003c/a\u003e. If you have pets and kids, it\u0026rsquo;s much harder to keep white cabinets looking clean. Dark kitchen cabinets allow you to clean less frequently, and it takes less effort to make your kitchen look tidy.\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eVersatile Style\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003eDark shades aren\u0026rsquo;t just for\u0026nbsp;\u003ca href=\"https://vevano.com/resource-center/modern-kitchen-ideas/\" target=\"_blank\"\u003emodern kitchens\u003c/a\u003e. Many interior design styles gain panache from darker colors.\u0026nbsp;\u003ca href=\"https://vevano.com/resource-center/modern-farmhouse-kitchen-design-ideas/\" target=\"_blank\"\u003eFarmhouse kitchens\u003c/a\u003e\u0026nbsp;look great with a darker wood island paired with a lighter countertop and subway tile backsplash. Contemporary kitchens benefit from dark grey cabinetry with clean lines and high contrasts. Dark brown wood cabinets evoke comfort and coziness in classic or traditional kitchens. The options are endless.\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003ch2\u003e\u003cbr /\u003e\nWhich Dark Cabinet Shade is Best for Your Kitchen?\u003c/h2\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003eThe \u0026ldquo;dark\u0026rdquo; in your dark cabinets comes from either a stain or paint. Both types can look similar from a distance, but with a stain, you notice the grain of the wood and other intricate details as you look closer, such as variations in the color. Choose a stained cabinet if you prefer seeing the unique grain of wood. But if you\u0026rsquo;d rather not see the wood grain, choose a painted cabinet in any shade for balanced and even color throughout.\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003eShades are also available in different colors from dark grey to dark brown. Grey is a slightly lighter tone in warm or cool shades. Brown is a warmer tone, reminiscent of\u003ca href=\"https://vevano.com/page/wood-kitchen-cabinet-collections/\"\u003e\u0026nbsp;\u003cu\u003ewood kitchen cabinets\u003c/u\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u0026nbsp;but with a darker, more modern ambiance.\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003ch2\u003e\u003cbr /\u003e\nWhat Countertops and Floors Go with Dark Cabinets?\u003c/h2\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003eFor dark cabinets, we recommend lighter colors for other elements in your kitchen. The contrast of light and dark is interesting and keeps the space from feeling too gloomy or dim.\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eCountertops:\u003c/strong\u003e\u0026nbsp;Nearly any countertop choice works well with dark cabinets, but lighter colors provide a nice contrast while medium colors blend well. Avoid overly dark countertops with dark cabinets, as both shades can make your kitchen feel smaller and crowded. Marble, quartz, or granite countertops are both ideal materials for your kitchen remodel.\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eWall Colors:\u003c/strong\u003e\u0026nbsp;Use color on your walls to highlight the beauty of your cabinets and countertops. This works best by using softer, lighter colors that make dark cabinets pop. You can also go with a bright splash of color. Pairing a dark cabinet with a fun blue, green, or yellow wall creates a fun atmosphere with high visual interest.\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eBacksplash:\u003c/strong\u003e\u0026nbsp;Backsplash ideas range from bright and colorful to plain and minimal. Your choice of kitchen backsplash provides a chance to highlight your style and personality. If you love farmhouse kitchens, choose a subway tile backsplash in a lighter color to contrast nicely with your dark cabinetry. Colorful accents such as a bright geometric tile or solid red are also fun ideas for your new kitchen.\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eFlooring:\u003c/strong\u003e\u0026nbsp;As with other elements in your kitchen, contrast is key. A lighter floor adds the ideal contrast with dark cabinets. LVT, hardwood, or tile all work well with dark\u0026nbsp;\u003ca href=\"https://vevano.com/resource-center/cabinet-door-styles-101/\" target=\"_blank\"\u003ecabinets of any style\u003c/a\u003e\u0026nbsp;and design.\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eLighting:\u003c/strong\u003e\u0026nbsp;Since dark colors absorb more light than they reflect, adding more lighting sources to brighten up your space is a great idea. Lights with glass shades or large multi-light fixtures are great additions. Under-cabinet lighting also brightens up counter space under wall cabinets to create a more open look.\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eAppliances:\u003c/strong\u003e\u0026nbsp;While contrast is often the goal with interior designs, a stark contrast can be too distracting. As such, most appliance colors and finishes work well with dark cabinets but be careful of the stark contrast created when pairing bright white appliances with dark cabinets. We recommend stainless steel appliances or other neutral colors if your cabinets are especially dark.\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003ch2\u003e\u003cbr /\u003e\nDark Cabinet Hardware Choices\u003c/h2\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003eChoosing cabinet hardware is a critical part of completing the look you want to achieve, as well as ensuring your cabinets are functional. When pairing the pulls and knobs with your dark cabinets, the style is less important than the finish. The shape and style are open to your personal aesthetics, but the finish is key towards determining whether the hardware goes with the dark color or not.\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003eThe right finish adds character and charm to a kitchen or bathroom while a poor match stands out, but not in a good way. We recommend finishes such as stainless steel, satin gold, oil-rubbed bronze, or antique pewter, as these add the right amount of polish and balance out your darker kitchen cabinetry with a lighter metal.\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003ch2\u003e\u003cbr /\u003e\nFAQs About Dark Kitchen Cabinets\u003c/h2\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003eHave some questions before you buy dark kitchen cupboards? We have answers and many different kitchen cabinet ideas for inspiration.\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003ch3\u003e\u003cbr /\u003e\nAre dark wood cabinets coming back?\u003c/h3\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003e\u003ca href=\"https://vevano.com/page/white-kitchen-cabinet-collections/\"\u003e\u003cu\u003eWhite kitchen cabinets\u003c/u\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u0026nbsp;are currently more popular than dark cabinets, but the darker look is coming back in modern and transitional kitchens. If you don\u0026rsquo;t like the look of a pristine white kitchen but still love trendsetting, a dark kitchen can get you there. Darker cabinets are increasing in popularity because they\u0026rsquo;re easier to care for and add sophistication where lighter paints and natural woods cannot.\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003eWhere light wood cabinets show more muck and wear-and-tear, darker cabinet colors hide scratches and grime more easily. They\u0026rsquo;re also incredibly chic as darker stains tend to look more custom and posher than standard white cabinets.\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003eWood cabinets themselves, however, are always in style, no matter the shade. Wood features a more pleasing grain than laminate or fiberboard, and comforting and warmer than stainless steel. Wood is a timeless, classic\u0026nbsp;\u003ca href=\"https://vevano.com/resource-center/cabinet-materials/\" target=\"_blank\"\u003ecabinet material\u003c/a\u003e\u0026nbsp;that works in kitchens of any style, from contemporary to farmhouse.\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003ch3\u003e\u003cbr /\u003e\nWould a small kitchen look good with dark cabinets?\u003c/h3\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003eUsually small kitchens look better in light cabinet colors, but with a few tricks, dark wood cabinets can look stunning in any size kitchen. While light kitchen cabinets have the benefit of reflecting more light (making a room look bigger) kitchens with dark cabinets need other elements to feel light and airy.\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003eSmall kitchens look good with dark cabinets when paired with light wall colors, a minimalist aesthetic, or light-colored countertops. The lighter elements reflect light and the contrast adds definition and style to small kitchens, where space to display d\u0026eacute;cor is at a premium. Choose gray cabinets rather than black cabinets to help your small kitchen feel less dim and crowded. Dark cabinets in a minimalist style keep your kitchen from looking cluttered and congested, instilling a sense of openness.\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003ch3\u003e\u003cbr /\u003e\nWhich dark cabinet is right for your kitchen?\u003c/h3\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003eThe right dark cabinet for your kitchen depends on your style and color preferences. Two of our favorite dark kitchen cabinets have opposite styles and shades. See how they compare to help you narrow down exactly what you love about dark wood kitchen cabinets.\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eWilora Paloma Marquis Dark Wood\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003eThis collection features\u003ca href=\"https://vevano.com/product/32035-mdw10x10-marquis-dark-wood-10x10-kitchen/\"\u003e\u0026nbsp;\u003cu\u003edark brown kitchen cabinets\u003c/u\u003e\u003c/a\u003e, with a modern frameless construction. The slab style doors and drawer fronts feature a beautiful dark chocolate wood grain texture. Ideal for modern kitchens, the Marquis Dark Wood cabinets pair well with simple hardware pulls, and metal light fixtures. If you prefer function over form, this collection is designed with storage in mind, the frameless construction allows for more storage space than its framed cabinet counterparts. They\u0026rsquo;re also made of engineered wood which is more water-resistant and warp-resistant than real wood.\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eWilora Hawthorne Shaker Cinder\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003eThis collection works well in modern or farmhouse kitchens. The more traditional frame style features a\u0026nbsp;\u003ca href=\"https://vevano.com/resource-center/cabinet-door-styles-101/\" target=\"_blank\"\u003eShaker style door\u003c/a\u003e\u0026nbsp;with rectangular frames and recessed panels. Each door and frame is stained with a classically comforting grey shade. These\u003ca href=\"https://vevano.com/product/32040-scc10x10-shaker-cinder-10x10-kitchen/\"\u003e\u0026nbsp;\u003cu\u003edark gray cabinets\u003c/u\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u0026nbsp;are slightly lighter than dark brown cabinets, so the wood grain is easier to see. If you love a farmhouse kitchen style, but don\u0026rsquo;t care for a hard to clean bright white cabinet, these shaker cabinets create the same look and feel, but with an easier-to-maintain surface.\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003ch3\u003e\u003cbr /\u003e\nHow can you brighten your kitchen with dark cabinets?\u003c/h3\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003eIf you love dark wood cabinets, but want a brighter kitchen, there are many design tips to create the ideal kitchen you\u0026rsquo;re looking for.\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eOpen shelving\u003c/strong\u003e: Opting for open shelving instead of traditional wall cabinets can make your kitchen space feel brighter and more open. This creates a gradient in your kitchen as colors get darker going from ceiling to floor (if you opt for a dark-colored floor as well).\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eUnder cabinet lighting\u003c/strong\u003e: Installing under-cabinet lighting adds light in places natural light rarely touches. Shining focused light on countertops and shelves both brightens and adds mood lighting to your kitchen. Other traditional lighting options are also a good idea, pendant lights over an island or recessed lights throughout your kitchen do so much to brighten up the space.\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eTwo-toned cabinets\u003c/strong\u003e: With this method, choose two different cabinet colors: one for the wall cabinets and one for your base cabinets. Traditionally, a darker color is reserved for the base cabinets and a lighter color for the upper cabinets. This lets you achieve the lush look of dark cabinetry but keeps your kitchen bright because the lighter tone of the wall cabinets reflects more light.\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003ch2\u003e\u003cbr /\u003e\nPersonalized\u0026nbsp;Design Service for Your Kitchen Cabinets\u003c/h2\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003eNot sure which style of dark cabinet to choose for your dream kitchen?
